   .Japanese DBCS, Code conversion.

#ifdef UNX

    #ifdef AIX
      SJIS(Shift-JIS). Browse and DBCS input are both avail.
    #endif

    #ifdef LNX
                                                                      ||~v124I~
      EUC-JP. Browse is avail under kon(Kanji ON console) if on the CONSOLE.||~v124R~
        DBCS input is not avail on kon,avail on X-terminal emulator   ||~v124R~
        such as gnome-terminal,kterm.                                 ||~v124I~
                                                                      ||~v124I~
      Hankaku-Katakana.                                               ||~v124I~
        SS2(0x8e)+xx(e.g 0x8eb1 pronounced "a") is 1 column width on display.||~v124I~
        RH9 binary treates those as unprintable.                      ||~v124I~||~v125R~
        From FC5 binary, those are displayed by 2 colomn(gxe) or Hankaku-Katakana+TABPAD(xe).||~v124I~||~v125R~
        TABPAD fills  spaces by tab(0x09) and controled to display by "TAB on /off" cmd||~v125R~
                                                                      ||~v124I~
      3 byte Kanji(SS3(0x8f)+xxxx) is displayed as 2 column Kanji+TABPAD,||~v125R~
                                                                      ||~v124I~
    #endif

#else
      SJIS(MS932) is applyed.                                         ||~v124R~
#endif

      CV command is for code conversion between SJIS,EUC,IBM-EBCDIC,
      unicode,UTF-8.
      Katakana and english lowercase letter is often mis-converted    ||~v124R~
      when EBCDIC to SJIS conversion. Those file may be re-converted  ||~v124R~
      each other.
      HEX notation to char conversion is also supported.
      To display comunication log by EBCDIC,for example,              ||~v124R~
      diaply all dump lines only by cmd "xx;f 0 1 all",               ||~v124R~
      then use "cv x2c ebc 5-80:100 mult nx".                         ||~v124R~
      Result of conversion of HEX-botation->CHAR(EBCDIC)->ASCII is written||~v124R~
      to from column 100.                                             ||~v124R~
      XCV cmd enclosed is external tool to file encoding translation. ||~v124I~
                                                                      ||~v124R~
#if defined(W32) || defined(LNX)                                      ||~v124R~
                                                                      ||~v124R~
   .EBCDIC file support.                                              ||~v125R~
                                                                      ||~v125R~
      (See also next section "EBCDIC translation" about CV cmd, XCV utility and EBCDIC cfg file)||~v125R~||~v125R~
                                                                      ||~v125R~
      -EBCDIC encoded file is maintained as it is without translation to locale codepage.||~v125R~
       Hex display mode displays EBCDIC code.                         ||~v125R~
       Use this function for the file downloaded from mainframe with no translation option||~v125R~
       or NFS mounted with no translation option.                     ||~v125R~
       It is usefull when asccessing Linux/390 using sshfs(Dokan sshfs on windows)||~v125I~
       Unicode is used to display code, it enable to dispaly wider range of printable character.||~v125R~
       Default EBCDIC converter is CP930 on Japanese environment and CP037 on the other env.||~v125I~
       This env is local env, specify proper converter on EBCDIC cfg file if remote env is||~v125I~
       diffrent from local.                                           ||~v125I~
       And also try to select other than default charset on setup dialog of wxe||~v125R~
       if invalid glyph is displayed.                                 ||~v125I~
                                                                      ||~v125R~
      -CPEB option is used for EDIt/SAVe/REPlace/CREate/APPend/CUT/END/COPy/MOVe/PASte cmd.||~v125R~
       IE option may be required if invalid EBCDIC code is contained. ||~v125R~
       Indicater on header line is "=E" , and "=e" when binary mode.  ||~v125R~
       (The file containing unprintable char with some extent is opened as binary file,||~v129R~
       and DBCS is not detected when binary mode. /Mt is option to force text mode.)||~v129R~
       LineFeed is 0x15 if /Mp(0x0d0a) or /Mu(0x0a) is not specified. ||~v129R~
         e.g. "e file1 cpeb"                                          ||~v125R~||~v128R~
       When cfg file is not prepared or to use different codepage than defined on cfg file,||~v125R~
       use CPEB:codepage format.                                      ||~v125R~
         e.g. "e file1 cpeb:IBM1047"                                   ||~v125R~||~v128R~
       Specify null like as "CPEB=" when back to cfg definition.      ||~v125R~
       xe accept max 7 codepages. xe can not recognize alias name.    ||~v125R~
                                                                      ||~v125R~
       COPy/MOVe/PASte cmd inserts lines after translated from specified codepage to the encoding of th opened file.||~v125R~
       SAVe/REPlace/CREate/APPend/CUT/END cmd write lines after translated to the specified codepage.||~v125R~
         e.g. "rep file2 cpeb nx ie"                                  ||~v125R~||~v128R~
                                                                      ||~v125R~
       CPEB:codepage option is available for these cmd.               ||~v125R~
       Specified option on output cmd is registered to profile.       ||~v125R~
       COPy/MOVe/PASte cmd checks profile, so you may not be required to specify CPxx option.||~v125R~
       But naming may differ between ICU and iconv/Windows codepage.  ||~v125R~
       So, when you changed CONVERTER parameter of cfg file between ICU and not ICU,||~v125R~
       codepage name on profile may invalid.  Paste may fail in that case.||~v125R~
       Re-specify CPEB parameter on Edit cmd for these case.          ||~v125R~
                                                                      ||~v125R~
       Even when CPEB is not spcified translation occures if codepage is registered to profile.||~v125R~
       Spevify "B"(Binary) suffix option if you do not want it.       ||~v125R~
       "B" option is not supported for UTF8 file as copy target.      ||~v125R~
       See "C"(Copy)/"M"(Move) lcmd for "B" suffix.                   ||~v125R~
                                                                      ||~v125R~
       Option specified to a directory is default for the file in the directory.||~v125R~
       To reset profile specify explicuitly other(CPLC/CPU8/CPAS) encoding option at open.||~v125R~
       EBCDIC codepage is displayed on the TopOfLine and EndOfLine.   ||~v125R~
                                                                      ||~v125R~
       Cmd for write dose not update profile if translation error is detected,||~v125R~||~v125R~
       file is written upto EOF replacing those error character to substitution character.||~v125R~
       Substitution character depends to the codepage, you can change it by cfg parameter.||~v125R~
       Sometimes DBCS subchar is not defined, xe try to translate u-fffd, u-ff1f(DBCS "?"),u-3000(DBCS space)||~v125R~
       in this sequence the use it if available.                      ||~v125R~
                                                                      ||~v125R~
      -"C"/"M" line cmd also execute translation when codepage differs.||~v125R~
       Spevify "B"(Binary) suffix option if you do not want it.       ||~v125R~
       "B" option is not supported for UTF8 file as both copy source and copy target.||~v125R~
       Spaces by Tab expansion is dropped when copy from locale code file to EBCDIC file.||~v125R~
         {A|B}[B][C][n][,b][.s]                                       ||~v125R~
           A : After, B: Before, B : Binary Mode, C : Copy with CID   ||~v125R~
           n : repeat, b : bandle, s : skip                           ||~v125R~
         e.g. c3                                                      ||~v125R~||~126FR~||~v128R~
              :       Copy 3 lines After by Binary mode               ||~v125R~
              ab                                                      ||~v125R~
                                                                      ||~v125R~
      -"="(Compare) line cmd compares the line after translated if the codepage differs.||~v125R~
       (EBCDIC file is translated to UTF8/Locale coed then compared)  ||~v125R~
       Use "B" suffix to compare by binary code.                      ||~v125R~
       Spaces by Tab expansion is ignored.                            ||~v125R~
         =[B][n][,b][.s]                                              ||~v125R~
         ==[B]                                                        ||~v125R~
         (supply "B" at any one of the line cmds)                     ||~v125R~
                                                                      ||~v125R~
      -CV cmd.                                                        ||~v125R~
                                                                      ||~v125R~
      -CV cmd B2M/M2B option is for CPLC(Locale code)file only.       ||~v125R~||~v125R~
       Cfg file is shared with EDIt cmd, -MFcfgfile option is discarded.||~v125R~||~v125R~
       CPEB:ebcdic-codepage parameter for B2M/M2B allows translation by out mapping cfg file specified on ini file.||~v125R~
       If CPEB is missing for the ebcidic file B2M uses the codepage of the opend file.||~v125R~
         e.g. cv m2b cpeb:37                                           ||~v125R~||~v128R~
       Use B2B option to translate between different EBCDIC codepage. ||~v125R~
         e.g. cv b2b cpeb:1026                                         ||~v125R~||~v128R~
       B2B without SETCP option dose not change the codepage of current file, the file is displayed using original||~v125R~
       codepage.                                                      ||~v125R~
       To change also the codepage itself, use SETCP option.          ||~v125R~
         e.g. cv b2b cpeb:1026 SETCP                                   ||~v125R~||~v128R~
                                                                      ||~v125R~
      -EBC cmd.                                                       ||~v125R~
                                                                      ||~v125R~
       EBC cmd also changes the codepage of the file.                 ||~v125R~
         e.g. EBC SETCP=CP935                                          ||~v125R~||~v128R~
       EBC cmd dose not change original code, but display the code according the codepage.||~v125R~
       So, close operation dose not write back to the file if there are no other modification to the file.||~v125R~
       Undo function restores SETCP effects of CV/EBC cmd.            ||~v125R~
       Codepage by SETCP option is registered to profile at close operation(not CANcel but END operation)||~v125R~
       Use "EBC SETCP=" to back to default codepage.                  ||~v127I~
                                                                      ||~v125R~
      -xcv utility.                                                   ||~v125R~
                                                                      ||~v125R~
         "m" of "m2b/b2m" is current codepage only, specify codepage for "b" using ebcmap file or -CPEB: option.||~126DI~
           e.g. xcv -cm2b -cpeb:37 -mseteol localfile1  ebcfile1       ||~v125R~||~v128R~
         To translate to the different EBCDIC codepage, use B2B option.||~v125R~
           e.g. xcv -cb2b -f:37 -t:1026 ebcfile1 -oebcfile2              ||~v125R~||~126DR~||~v128R~
         "-MF:" parameter is also required if use ICU converter. Specify CONVERTER=1 on the cfg file.||~v125R~
         Or spacify -ICU option.                                      ||~126DI~
           e.g. xcv -cb2b -f:IBM037 -t:IBM1047 -mf:xeebc.map ebcfile1 ebcfile2||~v125R~||~v128R~
                xcv -cb2b -f:IBM037 -t:IBM1047 -ICU          ebcfile1 ebcfile2||~126DI~||~v128R~
                                                                      ||~v125R~
      -EndOfLine-ID.                                                  ||~v125R~
       Supports not only RecordMode but also Text mode by EndOfLineID of 0x15(EBCDIC-NL).||~v125R~
       Default of EBCDIC file is text mode.                           ||~v125R~
       Following cmds has EOL related option. LRECL can be changed.   ||~v125R~
         EDIt/BROwse, END, CREate/REPlace, SAVe, COPy/MOVe.           ||~126FR~
       For SAVe cmd, new option is accepted when filename parameter is specified.||~v125R~
       For COPy/MOVe cmd Fxx option is LRECL of copy source file.     ||~v125R~
       RecordMod:On/Off and LRECL is saved to corresponding profile record,||~v125R~
       but EOL-ID is required each time.                              ||~v125R~
           /M{t|p|u|m|e|r} /Fnn[-mm]                                  ||~v125R~
             e:EBCDIC-NL(0x15), r;RecordMode, nn:LRECL                ||~v125R~
       e.g.                                                           ||~v125R~||~v128R~
           e ebcf1 CPEB                        : EBCDIC file TextMode(EOL-ID=0x15)||~v125R~
           e ebcf1 CPEB  /mp                   : EBCDIC file TextMode(EOL-ID:0x0d0a)||~v125R~
           e ebcf1 CPEB  /mr /F72              : EBCDIC file RecordMode(LRECL=72)||~v125R~
                                                 Default LRECL is 80. ||~v125R~
           end /mu                             : Change EOL-ID to 0x0a.||~v125R~
           end /mr /f80                        : Save as LRECL=80 RecordMode file(no EOL-ID).||~v125R~
           s ebcf1 CPEB /mr /F80               : translate (From PC file) to EBCDIC file.||~v125R~
                                                 Output is LRECL=80 RecordMode file.||~v125R~
           rep u8f1 nx CPU8 /mp                : translate (from RecordMode EBCDIC file) to UTF8 file.||~v125R~
                                                 EOL-ID:0x0d0a is appended to each line.||~v125R~
                                                                      ||~v125R~
      -About DBCS                                                     ||~v125R~
       Double Byte Character is indicated by SO(ShiftOut:0x0e) and SI(ShiftIn:0x0f) in EBCDIC.||~v125R~
       SO and SI enclose DBCS string. e.g. 0e-40-40-0f is DBCS space. ||~v125R~||~v128R~
       In other than EBCDIC, specific leading byte and some following bytes is combination of DBCS.||~v125R~
       Display width of DBCS is 2 column and it may be consists by 3 byte (EUC-SS3) or 3 byte(GB18030).||~v125R~
       e.g. DBCS space is 81-40 in MS932.                             ||~v125R~||~v128R~
       Accordingly translation between EBCDIC and Locale code changes line length if DBCS is contained.||~v125R~
       Option of treatement of SO/SI is prepared on translation cmd.  ||~v125R~
       Set default to cfg file.                                       ||~v125R~
       cfg option is applied to "C"opy line cmd which has no parameter for SI/SI option.||~v125R~
         e.g.  COPy     file1 cpeb -sd       :Delete SO/SI from EBCDIC copy source file. Line length will shrink.||~v125R~||~v128R~
               COPy     file1 cpeb -sr       :SO/SI is replaced to one space.||~v125R~
               REPlace  file1 cpeb -sr       :SO/SI is inserted at translation to EBCDIC,||~v125R~
                                              but replace both side of space if avail.||~v125R~
               REPlace  file1 cpeb -si       :SO/SI is inserted simply. Line length will expand.||~v125R~
       Define default action on cfg file.                             ||~v125R~
           SOSI_A2E      REP (="-sr") or INS ("=-si")                 ||~v125R~
           SOSI_E2A      DEL (="-sd") or REP ("=-sr")                 ||~v125R~
                                                                      ||~v125R~
      -Codepage and translation option by cfg file.                   ||~v125R~
         Specify cfg filename on INI file. Default is ::xeebc.cfg.    ||~v125R~
           EBCDIC_cfg        ="" #("::xeebc.map")# EBCDIC translation config filename||~v125R~
         Syntax is same as previously used for 3270 connection.       ||~v125R~
           Following option is added for non-3270 as alternative of option in xehosts file.||~v125R~
           This is for Windows/Japanese user with no external converter option only.||~v125R~
            SJIS_OPT  ENG_EXT      # Japanese English-Extension(CP939=CP1027)||~v125R~
            SJIS_OPT  KANA_EXT     # Japanese Katakana-Extension(CP930=CP290)||~v125R~
         -MF:mapfile option of CV cmd for B2M/M2B was discarded,      ||~v125R~
         CV cmd share mapping option specified on INI file.           ||~v125R~
         Default option when missing cfg file is as following.        ||~v125R~
           (Windows)                                                  ||~v125R~
             Japanese :Codepage=CP930(Internal mapping table equivalent to Japanese-Katakana Extension), JIS83.||~v125R~
             else     :Codepage=CP037, No DBCS(SO/SI) consideration.  ||~v125R~
           (Linux)                                                    ||~v125R~
             Japanese :Codepage=EUC-JP(Internal mapping table equivalent to Japanese-Katakana Extension), JIS83.||~v125R~
             else     :Codepage=CP037, No DBCS(SO/SI) consideration.  ||~v125R~
           Above default is used when CONVERTER=0 on cfg file, you can specify additional option||~v125R~
           such as SOSI,SJIS option.                                  ||~v125R~
           SOSI option is effective for CV cmd only, ignored for EDIt operation.||~v125R~
                                                                      ||~v125R~
         (e.g.)sample to use External(ICU/iconv) converter, Windows codepage.||~v126R~||~v128R~
               On Windows, you may have to add the EBCDIC codepage using||~v125R~
                 Control-Panel-->Region and Languages                 ||~v125R~
               WindowsXP currently have no EBCDIC codepage supporting DBCS.||~v125R~
               So, CJK user may have to install ICU to use DBCS EBCDIC. (COVERTER=0 supports Japanese)||~v125R~
               To use ICU you may have to set PATH for DLL/so. Set PATH(LIBPATH is not used) or LD_LIBRARY_PATH.||~v126R~
                                                                      ||~v125R~
               Codepage value on CHARSET statement varies by ICU/Windows/LinuxICONV.||~v125R~
               Confirm it using "uconv -l" (ICU) or "iconv -l".       ||~v125R~
               For codepage on Windows, check it by Control-panel-->Region and Language.||~v125R~
                                                                      ||~v125R~
               -Use ICU SBCS.                                         ||~v125R~
                  CONVERTER          1                                ||~v125R~
                  ICU_DLL_SUFFIX    44                                ||~v125R~
                  ICU_API_SUFFIX   _44                                ||~v125R~
                  SBCS_CHARSET     cp1047          //EBCDIC Latin/1 Open System(iso-8859-1)||~v125R~
                                                                      ||~v125R~
               -Use ICU DBCS.                                         ||~v125R~
                  CONVERTER          1                                ||~v125R~
                  ICU_DLL_SUFFIX    44                                ||~v125R~
                  ICU_API_SUFFIX   _44                                ||~v125R~
                  DBCS_CHARSET     cp1388          //chinese simplified. superset of cp935||~v125R~
                                                                      ||~v125R~
               -Use Windows MultiByteToWideChar/WideCharToMultibute API.||~v125R~
                  CONVERTER          2                                ||~v125R~
                  SBCS_CHARSET       20924        //EBCDIC Latin/1 Open System(1047+Euro)||~v125R~
                                                                      ||~v125R~
               -Use Linux iconv API.                                  ||~v125R~
                  CONVERTER          2                                ||~v125R~
                  SBCS_CHARSET       cp1047                           ||~v125R~
                                                                      ||~v125R~
         Translation of EndOfLine ID may not be preferable.           ||~v125R~
             EBCDIC NL(x15)-->u0085, LF(x25)-->u000a                  ||~v125R~
             ASCII  LF(0x0a)-->EBC-15/EBC-25                          ||~v125R~
         You can remap it as following.                               ||~v125R~
             MAP_E2A  0x15: 0x0a   # EBCDIC 0x15(NL) -> ASCII 0a(LF)  ||~v125R~
             MAP_E2A  0x25: 0x3b   # EBCDIC 0x25(LF) -> ASCII "?"     ||~v125R~
             MAP_A2E  0x0a: 0x15   # EBCDIC 0x15(NL) <- ASCII 0a(LF)  ||~v125R~
                                                                      ||~v125R~
                                                                      ||~v125R~
                                                                      ||~v125R~
      -0x09 is not TAB (0x05:EBC-HT also is  not treated as TAB skip character).||~v125R~
       When Tab Key is pressed, TAB char(0x09,0x05) is not inserted into the line,||~v125R~
       but jump some columns even when INS mode.                      ||~v125R~
      -HEX input mode(Ctrl+F11) send byte by byte(no DBCS consideration)||~v125R~
      -SO(0x0e)/SI(0x0f)(DBCS encloser) is displayed by alternative char "?".||~v125R~
       SO/SI is inserted when DBCS kbd input.                         ||~v125R~
       For Cut&Paste DBCS re-evaluation is done each time.            ||~v125R~
       DBCS is even byte string enclosed by SO and SI.                ||~v125R~
       For ex, when paste EBCDIC line into UTF8/Locale code file,     ||~v125R~
       Translation will be done but unless SO/SI is not included in the pasteing data||~v125R~
       DBCS translation is not done and SBCS translation is done.     ||~v125R~
       When Joined 2 line split at DBCS position, DBCS may revive.    ||~v125R~
       TFLow cmd also join line but insert single space between the line joined,||~v125R~
       so DBCS may not revive.                                        ||~v125R~
       Invalid DBCS-EBCDIC is displayed by ":;", confirm the code by vertical hex line.||~v125R~
      -Binary mode by EB cmd or by the reason that file contains too may control char||~v125R~
       dose not consider DBCS. Use ET cmd for later case.             ||~v125R~
      -Find/Change cmd.                                               ||~v125R~
         Regardless of kbd mode is UTF8 or not, search and replace by EBCDI Code on EBCDIC file.||~v125R~
         No DBCS consideration for the file opened by binary mode.    ||~v125R~
         -g (Grep), P'.' option is not supported.                     ||~v125R~
      - "#" line cmd(Execute cmd descripted on the line) is not supported.||~v125R~
                                                                      ||~v125R~
   .EBCDIC translation.                                               ||~v124R~
                                                                      ||~v124R~
      You can use external converter such as ICU/iconv for EBCDIC translation.||~v124R~
      CV cmd(XCV is embedded tool for translation) and xe3270 FTP utilize those converter.||~v124R~
      Prepare parameter file for it, followings are description for the parameter file.||~v124R~
      (See "EBCDIC file support" about editting direct EBCDIC file.)  ||~v125R~
                                                                      ||~v124R~
      ****************************************************************************||~v124R~
                                                                      ||~v124R~
        This file defines EBCDIC translation parameter                ||~v124R~
        which is use for EBCDIC fiel support, CV edit cmd, xe3270 FTP, XCV utility.||~v125R~
        Links to this file is CHARSET_CFG parameter in the xe3270.cfg for xe3270 FTP,||~v124R~||~v125R~
        /MF:mapfile parameter for XCV cmd.                    ||~v124R~||~v125R~
        For EBCDIC file support and CV edit cmd, specify on INI file. ||~v125R~
            EBCDIC_cfg   ="" #("::xeebc.map")# EBCDIC translation config filename||~v125R~
                                                                      ||~v124R~
        There are 3 translation pattern.                              ||~v124R~
         Other than required parameter for each case is ignored.      ||~v124R~
         (a). Japanese translation using internal mapping table.      ||~v124R~
              XCV and CV cmd has related parameter and those are adopted if specified.||~v124R~
              For xe3270 FTP, you can specify those parameters in this file if required.||~v124R~
              SJIS_OPT, SOSI_A2E and SOSI_E2A are the only effective parameters.||~v124R~
         (b). Translation using external(ICU) or system(Windows NLS API or Linux iconv) converter.||~v124R~
              You may use standalone tool,uconv of ICU or iconv of Linux.||~v124R~
              Use this file to use these converter in xe3270 FTP.     ||~v124R~
              This file may be used from CV and XCV cmd to adjust translation by those converter.||~v124R~
              MAP_A2E/MAP_E2A is applied to the specific codepoint.   ||~v124R~
              You can get the list of charset by "uconv -l" (ICU), "iconv -l"(iconv).    ||~v124R~||~v125R~
              List of codepage of Windows or ICU converter is gotton by "xcv -List"||~126DR~
              (It seems to be no DBCS EBCDIC codepage in Windows,     ||~v124R~
               ICU will be required for DBCS user if pattern (a) above is not proper).||~v124I~
         (c). Apply mapping after and downlowd and before upload by s3270+IND$FILE transfer.||~v124R~
              MAP_A2F is applied before upload and MAP_F2A is applied after download||~v124R~
              to adjust the s3270 translation.                        ||~v124R~
              Other option than MAP_A2F and MAP_F2A are ignored.      ||~v124R~
                                                                      ||~v124R~
        About 3270 FTP.                                               ||~v124R~
          .For DBCS user.                                             ||~v124R~
              IND$FILE dose not support DBCS(DoubleByteCharSet) translation.||~v124R~
              (s3270 made by --enable-DBCS option translates screen data only.)||~v124R~
              So, xe3270 translates FTP data using internal/external converter, then send/receive by binaly mode.||~v124R~
              (Binary mode is a little bit faster than text mode transfer).||~v124I~
              It supports fixed-record-length DATASET MEMBER only.    ||~v124R~
              For variable-record length DATASET(MEMBER) SBCS translation is applied,||~v124R~
              and you can adjust it using (c) of above.               ||~v124R~
                                                                      ||~v124R~
              And, you have to specify DBCS= option in the xehosts file.||~v124R~
              If DBCS=CP939 or DBCS=CP930, xe3270 uses internal translation table.(pattern(a))||~v124R~
                                                                      ||~v124R~
              If DBCS=OTHER and CONVERTER=1, xe3270 uses external/system converter(case(b)).||~v124R~
              Parameters in this file are applied as following.       ||~v124R~
                Upload to host.                                       ||~v124R~
                  [PCcode]->{mbrtowc/LOCAL_CHARSET}->[UCS2]->{DBCS_CHARSET/SBCS_CHARSET}->[EBCDIC]||~v124R~
                        ===>(binary mode xfer)===>HOST                ||~v124R~
                Download from host                                    ||~v124R~
                  [PCcode]<-{wcrtomb/LOCAL_CHARSET}<-[UCS2]<-{DBCS_CHARSET/SBCS_CHARSET}<-[EBCDIC]||~v124R~
                        <===(binary mode xfer)<===HOST                ||~v124R~
              MAP_A2E,MAP_E2A and SUBCHAR_xxx options are used to adjusts SBCS translation.||~v124R~
              Codepoints defined there are mapped without using converter.||~v124R~
                                                                      ||~v124R~
          .For SBCS user.                                             ||~v124R~
              s3270 supports some translation tabe by --charset option.||~v124R~
              (See http://x3270.bgp.nu/s3270-man.html for supported charset)||~v124R~
              It seems there are no need to install external converter for s3270 FTP.||~v124R~
              If there are some code points which dose not fit to your environments,||~v124R~
              use MAP_F2A and MAP_A2F with CONVERTER=0(case (c)).     ||~v124R~
              Parameters in this file are applied as following.       ||~v124R~
                Upload to host.                                       ||~v124R~
                  [PCcode]->{MAP_A2F}->[PCcode]->(s3270)->[PCcode]===>(IND$FILE)->[EBCDIC]||~v124R~
                Download from host                                    ||~v124R~
                  [PCcode]<-{MAP_F2A}<-[PCcode]<-(s3270)<===[PCcode]<-(IND$FILE)<-[EBCDIC]||~v124R~
                                                                      ||~v124R~
              You can also use SBCS_CHARSET and MAP_A2E/MAP_E2A for fixed-record-length DATASET MEMBER.||~v124R~
              If CONVERTER=1 and and SBCS_CHARSET is specified,       ||~v124R~
              SBCS translation is done like as DBCS translation for fixed-record-length DATASET MEMBER..||~v124R~
              If SBCS_CHARSET is DEFAULTMAP, translation is done without using converter||~v124R~
              by mapping table same as of s3270(ISO-8859-1 and CP037).||~v124R~
                                                                      ||~v124R~
        About Fixed-Record-Length.                                    ||~v124R~
          When DATASET's RECFM attribute is fixed for xe3270 FTP,     ||~v124R~
          when /F[xx][N] cmdline option is specified for XCV cmd,(No Fixed option for CV cmd)||~v124R~
          long lines are split and short lines are expanded at translation to EBCDIC.||~v124R~
          NO EndOfLineID(0x0a) is written(XCV cmd support /Mseteol option).||~v124R~
          "N" option means last 8 byte of line-number-field.          ||~v124R~
          Expanded line by insertion of SO/SI for DBCS is shrinked    ||~v124R~
          to the LRECL if space is available before the line-number-field.||~v124R~
          The line number field overflowed the LRECL will be cut if "N" specified.||~v124R~
          For xe3270 FTP, set profile:NUMSTD by PRO cmd.              ||~v124R~
          (Open a MENBER with /Mn option,then enter "PRO path save")  ||~v124R~
                                                                      ||~v124R~
          When translated from EBCDIC,lines are read by binary mode(0x0a is also translated)||~v124R~
          and EOL-ID is written.                                      ||~v124R~
                                                                      ||~v124R~
        By /Mseteol option of XCV cmd EOL-ID is append to each line for both To and From EBCDIC case.||~v124R~||~v125R~
            /mASCEOL: EOL-ID of EBCDIC file is Windows:0x0d0a, Linux 0x0a. Default is 0x15.||~v125R~
            /mSETEOL: EOL-ID is appended to each output line. for x2B and B2x with RecordMode.||~v125R~
          (                                                           ||~v125R~
           Specify LRECL by /Fxx option                               ||~v125R~
              /F[nn][N]:EBCDIC file is fixed record length. nn:LRECL(default=80).||~v125R~
                        Input(B2x) or Output(x2B) LRECL.              ||~v125R~
                        N: last 8 byte is line-number-filed. adjust SO/SI insertion.||~v125R~
                           "N" is effective for m2b only.             ||~v125R~
          )                                                           ||~v125R~
          e.g.                                                        ||~v125R~||~v128R~
           xcv /cm2b ms932 ibm939.txt  /mf:sjisebc.map /F80 /Mseteol /Masceol||~v125R~
               (locale-->ebcdic, output LRECL=80, set ASCII-EOL-ID)   ||~v125R~
           xcv /cm2b ms932 ibm939.txt /mf:sjisebc.map  /Masceol /Mseteol||~v125R~
               (locale-->ebcdic, output line with appened ASCII-EOL-ID)||~v125R~
           xcv /cb2m ebcf1 ascf2 /mf:sjisebc.map /F80 /Mseteol        ||~v125R~
               (locale<--ebcdic, input LRECL=80, output line with appened ASCII-EOL-ID)||~v125R~
           xcv /cb2m ebcf1 ascf2 /mf:sjisebc.map /Masceol             ||~v125R~
               (locale<--ebcdic, input line with ASCII-EOL-ID         ||~v125R~
                                                                      ||~v124R~
      ## sample file ##                                               ||~v124R~
                                                                      ||~v124R~
        xeebc.map                                                     ~
        ##################################################################################
        #                                                             
        #   CONVERTER      : Converter selection                      
        #                    0 : SBCS translation by MAP_A2F and MAP_F2A mapping
        #                        Other option than MAP_A2F and MAP_F2A will be ignored.
        #                    1 : converter is ICU (ICU instalation is required)
        #                    2 : converter is iconv(Linux) or WideCharToMultibyte/MultiByteToWideChar(Windows)
        #                                                             
        #                    For 1 and 2, apply CHARSET_DBCS, CHARSET_DBCS (LOCAL_CHARSET)
        #                    with  optional adjustment by MAP_E2A and MAP_A2E.
        #                    MAP_A2F and MAP_F2A will be ignored.     
        #                      sample                                 
        #                         CONVERTER   1           # apply converter
        #   ICU_DLL_SUFFIX : .dll/.so library name sufix.             
        #                    This is required if "CONVERTER 1".       
        #                    Required when following default is not proper.||~v126R~
        #                       Android     : /system/lib             ||~v126R~
        #                       Linux       : /usr/local/lib:usr/lib:$(LD_LIBRARY_PATH)||~v126R~
        #                       Linux-64    : /usr/local/lib64:usr/lib64:$(LD_LIBRARY_PATH)||~v126R~
        #                       Windows     : GetSystemDirectory();GetWindowsDirectory();$(PATH)||~v126R~
        #                                     e.g.    GetSystemDirectory() : c:\Windows\system32||~v126R~||~v128R~
		#   									      GetWindowsDirectory(): c:\Windows||~v126R~
        #                      sample                                 
        #                         ICU_DLL_SUFFIX 44          # if dllname is icuuc40.dll||~v125R~
        #   ICU_API_SUFFIX : ICU api name sufix.                      
        #                    This is required if "CONVERTER 1".       
        #                    Required when default dll/so library is not available.||~v126R~
        #                    For ex, real name of "ucnv_open" is ucnv_open_4_0 on icuuc40.dll||~126DR~
        #                      sample                                 
        #                         ICU_DLL_SUFFIX _44        # if dllname is icuuc40.dll||~v125R~
        #                    See followings if you have source package.(ICU v44)||~v125R~
        #                         $(icu)/source/common/unicode/uvernum.h||~v125R~
		#		                      #define        U_ICU_VERSION_SHORT         "44"||~v125R~
		#			                  #define        U_ICU_ENTRY_POINT_RENAME(x)  x ## _44||~v125R~
        #                                                             
        #   ICU_DATA       : Use when you installed your own converter(.cnv file)||~126DI~
        #                     e.g.(Linux)   ICU_DATA /system/usr/icu:/data/data/yourcnvs||~126DI~||~v128R~||~v128R~||~v129R~
        #                         (Windows) ICU_DATA w:\icu\icu562\icu\bin;w:\icu\icu481\icu\bin||~v128R~||~v128R~||~v129R~
        #                    Put your cnv file into sub-folder yourcnvs/icudt__l  ; __ is version like as icudt44l.||~126DI~
        #                    (Windows) search ICU library(dll) also in ICU_DATA folder and in ICU_DATA enviromnent variable.||~v129R~
        #                    (Linux) set path to the .so to LD_LIBRARY_PATH.||~v129R~
        #                                                             ||~126DI~
        #   DBCS_CHARSET   : Defines EBCDIC charset name to translate UCS<-->EBCDIC which supports DBCS.||~v125R~
        #                    You can get the list of charset by "uconv -l" (ICU), "iconv -l"(iconv).||~v125R~
        #                    If missing this parameter All chars are translated byte by byte.
        #                    (Note) DBCS=OTHER parameter in the xehosts file is required for xe3270 FTP.
        #                      sample                                 
        #                         DBCS_CHARSET cp939     #Jpanese     ||~v124I~
        #                         DBCS_CHARSET cp933     #Korean Mixed EBCDIC||~v124I~
        #                         DBCS_CHARSET cp935     #Chinese(Simplified) Mixed EBCDIC||~v124I~
        #                         DBCS_CHARSET cp937     #Chinese(Traditional)Mixed EBCDIC||~v124I~
        #   SBCS_CHARSET   : Defines EBCDIC charset name to translate UCS2<-->EBCDIC
        #                    You can get the list of charset by "uconv -l" (ICU), "iconv -l"(iconv).||~v125R~
        #                    If DBCS_CHARSET can translate also SBCS,no need to specify SBCS_CHARSET.
        #                    "DEFAULTMAP" means to use internal mapping table cotrresponding to
        #                    iso8859-1<-->EBCDIC US same as IBM37,swaplfnl.||~126DR~
        #                    ibm37,swaplfnl is s390 standard.         ||~126DR~
        #                      EBCDIC-0x25<-->ASCII-0x85, EBCDIC-0x15<-->ASCII<-->0x0a||~126DR~
        #                      sample                                 
        #                         SBCS_CHARSET CP037          #use external converter
        #                         SBCS_CHARSET DEFAULTMAP     #use internal map corresponding to ISO-8859-1 and CP037
        #                      For CONVERTER=2 on Windows.            ||~v127I~
        #                        SBCS_CHARSET 1047           #EBCDIC latin||~v127I~
        #   LOCAL_CHARSET  : defines local charset name to translate UCS2<-->local codepage
        #                    If SBCS_CHARSET is DEFAULTMAP,this parameter is ignored
        #                    If missing, Codepage is determined by environment valiable(LANG,codepage).||~v125R~
        #                    For Axe, ICU is used.                    ||~v126R~
        #                      sample                                 
        #                         LOCAL_CHARSET ISO-8859-1     #use external converter
        #                         LOCAL_CHARSET SHIFT_JISX0213 #for iconv,0xe0-0xfc is not DBCS if "SJIS" is specified
        #                      Specify CodePage Number on Windows.    ||~v127I~
        #                        LOCAL_CHARSET   932          #JP     ||~v127I~
        #   MAP_E2A/MAP_A2E: mapping to adjust SBCS translation for each codepoint.
        #                    For ex,. 0x7e is tilde on iso-8859-1 upper-bar on cp897.
        #                    And 0xa0 is upper-bar and 0xa1 is tilede on CP1027(EBCDIC),
        #                    0xa1 is upper-bar and 0xa0 is tilede on cp290(EBCDIC),
        #                    When CP1027 is not supported by s3270 specify as following
        #                    with "s3270 -charset CP290"              
        #                      sample                                 
        #                         MAP_E2A  0xa0: 0xaf   # EBCDIC 0xa0 -> ASCII upper-bar
        #                         MAP_E2A  0xa1: ~      # EBCDIC 0xa1 -> ASCII tilde
        #                         MAP_A2E  0xaf: 0xa0   # EBCDIC 0xa0 <- ASCII upper-bar
        #                         MAP_A2E     ~: 0xa1   # EBCDIC 0xa1 <- ASCII tilde
        #   MAP_A2F/MAP_F2A: Effective for 3270 FTP case (c) only.    
        #                    For the purpose of adjusting translation by s3270+IND$FILE
        #                    MAP_A2F is applied to ASCII file to be upload to host,
        #                    MAP_F2A is applied to ASCII data downloaded from host.
        #                      sample                                 
        #                         MAP_A2F  0xaf: ~      # upload 0xaf(upper bar) as 0x7e(tilde)
        #                         MAP_F2A  0x1f: .      # convert downloaded 0x1f to printable char
        #   SUCHAR_SBCS    : substitution charscter by unicode for the case single byte translation error.
        #                    default is U001a.                        
        #   SUCHAR_DBCS    : substitution charscter by unicode for the case double byte translation error.
        #                    default is Ufffd.                        
        #                    ICU subchar of codepage->unicode translation is fixed to 0x1a and 0xfffd.
        #                    ICU subchar of codepage<-unicode translation is defined on each .ucm file of ICU.
        #                    xe accept both for EBCDIC<->unicode  and local codepage<->unicode if specifed.
        #                    So,SUBCHAR_SBCS and SUBCHAR_DBCS is applied to following 2 case.
        #                      LOCAL_CHARSET is not specified.(wcr2mb and mbrtowc are used)
        #                      "CONVERTER 2" is specified.(system converters are used)
        #                    If xe detected error, output is result of translation of this substitution char.
        #                      sample                                 
        #                         SUBCHAR_SBCS  0x003f       # "?" for translation err
        #                         SUBCHAR_DBCS  0x30fb       # EBCDIC 0x4345 in CP939
        #                    For other than ICU, default value Ufffd and U001a may not be valid for the codepage.
        #                    In those case original code will be left. You would be better to
        #                    specify SUBCHAR_xxxx parameter.          
        #   SUBCHAR_0a     : control converter's output 0x0a when translate to pc-codepage.
        #                    1 : replace by SBCS substitution char.   
        #                    0 : output 0x0a. (Default)               
        #   SUBCHAR_S2D    : replace converter output by substitution char when SBCS is translated to pc-codepage DBCS.
        #                    1 : replace by SBCS substitution char.   
        #                    0 : allow multibyte output. (Default)    
        #   SJIS_OPT       : Specify options for SJIS(japanese) translation.
        #                    Effective only for case (a) of xe3270 FTP(for the case DBCS=CP939 or CP930 in the xehosts file)
        #                    For CV and XCV cmd, cmdline parameter override this parameter.
        #                    IBM  :map EBCDIC kanji to SJIS-IBM area (Default)
        #                    NEC  :map EBCDIC kanji to SJIS-NEC area  
        #                    JIS78:SJIS 1978 version                  
        #                    JIS83:SJIS 1983 version (Default)        
        #                    ENG_EXT :Japanese English Extension(CP939=CP1027)||~v125R~
        #                    KANA_EXT:Japanese katakana Extension(CP930=CP290)||~v125R~
        #                      sample                                 
        #                         SJIS_OPT      NEC                   
        #                         SJIS_OPT      JIS78                 
        #                         SJIS_OPT      KANA_EXT              ||~v125R~
        #   SOSI_A2E       : SO/SI setting option when translate DBCS to EBCDIC
        #                    It can be overridden command option of CV/XCV/SAVe/REPlace/COPy/... cmd.||~v125R~
        #                    Default is SHIFT for xe3270 FTP, INS for the else.||~v125R~
        #                                                             ||~v125R~
        #                    INS  :insert SO(0xe) and SI(0x0f) enclosing DBCS string. Output may expand.
        #                    REP  :replace boundary space if exist, else insert.
        #                    SHIFT:(xe3270 Only) more over REP operation, delete following space by the inserted count.||~v125R~
        #                      sample                                 
        #                         SOSI_A2E      REP                   ||~v125R~
        #   SOSI_E2A       : SO/SI treatement when translate DBCS from EBCDIC
        #                    It can be overridden command option of CV/XCV/SAVe/REPlace/COPy/... cmd.||~v125R~
        #                                                             ||~v125R~
        #                    DEL  :delete SO and SI. Output may shrink.
        #                    REP  :replace SO and SI by ASCII space. (Default)
        #                                                             
        ##########################################################    
        # CONVERTER             1     # 0:s3270 translation, 1:ICU, 2:iconv/WindowsAPI||+v124R
        # ICU_DLL_SUFFIX      44      # ICU dllname suffix            ||~v125R~
        # ICU_API_SUFFIX      _44     # ICU apiname suffix            ||~v125R~
        # DBCS_CHARSET        cp939   #(Linux)EBCDIC Japanese English lower-case letter extension.~||+v124R
        # DBCS_CHARSET        nnnn    #(Windows)No corresponding Windows Codepage||+v124I
        # SBCS_CHARSET        cp037   #(Linux)EBCDIC-US               ||+v124R
        # SBCS_CHARSET        cp939                                   
        # SBCS_CHARSET        CP037   #Linux                          
        # SBCS_CHARSET        37      #Windows Codepage for CP037(EBCDIC US)
        # LOCAL_CHARSET    ISO-8859-1 #(Linux)Latin-1                 ||+v124R
        # LOCAL_CHARSET    28591      #(Windows Codepage) for ISO-8859-1||+v124R
        #                                                             
        #     MAP_A2F    0xaf: ~      # upload 0xaf(upper bar) as 0x7e(tilde)
        #     MAP_A2F    0x30: 0x31   # upload 0xaf(upper bar) as 0x7e(tilde)
        #     MAP_A2F    0x31: 0x30   # upload 0xaf(upper bar) as 0x7e(tilde)
        #     MAP_F2A    0x1f: .      # convert downloaded 0x1f to printable char
        #     MAP_F2A    0x31: 0x30   # upload 0xaf(upper bar) as 0x7e(tilde)
        #     MAP_F2A    0x30: 0x31   # upload 0xaf(upper bar) as 0x7e(tilde)
        #     MAP_F2A       {: }      # upload 0xaf(upper bar) as 0x7e(tilde)
        #     MAP_F2A       }: {      # upload 0xaf(upper bar) as 0x7e(tilde)
        #                                                             
        #     MAP_E2A    0xa2: 0x5c   # Yen sign and backslash        
        #     MAP_A2E    0x5c: 0xa2   #                               
        #     MAP_E2A    0xa1: ~      # tilde and upper bar           
        #     MAP_A2E       ~: 0xa1   #                               
        #     MAP_E2A    0xa0: ?      # tilde and upper bar           
        #                                                             
        #     MAP_E2A    0x25: ?      # avoid 0x0a generation         
        #     MAP_E2A    0x4a: ?      # Cent, avoid DBCS output by CP939
        #     MAP_E2A    0x5f: ?      # Not , avoid DBCS output by CP939
        #     MAP_E2A    0xb1: ?      # Pond, avoid DBCS output by CP939
        #                                                             
        #     MAP_E2A    0x31: 1      # Pond, avoid DBCS output by CP939
        #     MAP_E2A    0x32: 2      # Pond, avoid DBCS output by CP939
        #     MAP_E2A    0x33: 3      # Pond, avoid DBCS output by CP939
        #                                                             
        #   SOSI_A2E   INS : SOSI setting option when translate DBCS to EBCDIC
        #   SUBCHAR_DBCS    0x30fb                                    
        #   SUBCHAR_SBCS    0x1a                                      
        #   SUBCHAR_0a     1  # replace by SBCS substitution char.    
        #   SUBCHAR_S2D    1  # replace converter output by substitution char when SBCS is translated to pc-codepage DBCS.
        ##################################################################################||~v124R
        #                                                             ||~v125R~
        ## Use ICU , SBCS codepage                                    ||~v125R~
        #                                                             ||~v125R~
        #        CONVERTER          1                                 ||~v125R~
        #        ICU_DLL_SUFFIX    44                                 ||~v125R~
        #        ICU_API_SUFFIX   _44                                 ||~v125R~
        #        SBCS_CHARSET     cp1047          //EBCDIC Latin/1 Open System(iso-8859-1)||~v125R~
        #                                                             ||~v125R~
        ## Use ICU , DBCS codepage                                    ||~v125R~

        #        DBCS_CHARSET     cp1388          //chinese simplified. superset of cp935||~v125R~
